Authorization Implementation Summary\\n\\n## Overview\\nThe Kubernetes RBAC authorization system is implemented across multiple packages in the kubernetes/kubernetes repository, providing a comprehensive role-based access control mechanism for API requests.\\n\\n## Core Components\\n\\n### 1. RBACAuthorizer (plugin/pkg/auth/authorizer/rbac/rbac.go)\\nThe main authorizer component that implements the `authorizer.Authorizer` interface. Key aspects:\\n- **RBACAuthorizer struct** (line 50): Contains an `authorizationRuleResolver` field of type `RequestToRuleMapper`\\n- **Authorize method** (line 75): Evaluates whether a request is allowed by visiting applicable policy rules using an `authorizingVisitor`\\n- **RequestToRuleMapper interface** (line 37): Defines the contract for resolving policy rules (RulesFor and VisitRulesFor methods)\\n- **RuleAllows function** (line 178): Checks if a specific rule matches request attributes (verb, APIGroup, resource, resource names, non-resource URLs)\\n- **New function** (line 159): Factory method that creates a RBACAuthorizer with a DefaultRuleResolver\\n- **RulesFor method** (line 129): Converts policy rules to authorizer rule info for admin-facing operations\\n\\n### 2. SubjectAccessEvaluator (plugin/pkg/auth/authorizer/rbac/subject_locator.go)\\nComponent that evaluates which subjects (users/groups) can perform specific actions. Key aspects:\\n- **SubjectAccessEvaluator struct** (line 42): Contains role/rolebinding listers and a RoleToRuleMapper\\n- **NewSubjectAccessEvaluator function** (line 50): Creates evaluator with role/rolebinding data sources\\n- **AllowedSubjects method** (line 64): Returns subjects that can perform an action by checking cluster-wide and namespace-scoped bindings\\n- **RoleToRuleMapper interface** (line 30): For resolving role references to policy rules\\n\\n### 3. DefaultRuleResolver (pkg/registry/rbac/validation/rule.go)\\nThe core rule resolution engine that maps users to applicable policy rules. Key aspects:\\n- **DefaultRuleResolver struct** (line 91): Contains role/rolebinding getters and cluster role/rolebinding listers\\n- **NewDefaultRuleResolver function** (line 98): Factory for creating rule resolvers\\n- **AuthorizationRuleResolver interface** (line 37): Defines contract with methods GetRoleReferenceRules, RulesFor, and VisitRulesFor\\n- **RulesFor method** (line 118): Returns all policy rules applicable to a user in a namespace by accumulating rules via visitor pattern\\n- **VisitRulesFor method** (line 179): Visits each applicable rule by checking cluster role bindings and namespace-scoped role bindings\\n- **GetRoleReferenceRules method** (line 240): Resolves a RoleBinding/ClusterRoleBinding reference to its actual policy rules (distinguishes between Role and ClusterRole)\\n\\n### 4. SubjectAccessReview REST Handler (pkg/registry/authorization/subjectaccessreview/rest.go)\\nHTTP endpoint for checking authorization decisions. Key aspects:\\n- **REST struct** (line 35): Contains an authorizer field\\n- **NewREST function** (line 39): Factory for creating the REST handler\\n- **Create method** (line 63): Handles SubjectAccessReview requests by:\\n  - Validating the review spec\\n  - Converting spec to authorization attributes\\n  - Calling authorizer.Authorize\\n  - Returning decision (Allowed/Denied) and reason\\n\\n### 5. Bootstrap RBAC Policies\\nDefault RBAC roles and bindings created at cluster startup:\\n\\n**policy.go** (plugin/pkg/auth/authorizer/rbac/bootstrappolicy/policy.go):\\n- Defines standard cluster roles (system:masters, system:nodes, system:authenticated, etc.)\\n- Contains helper functions and verb constants (Read, Write, ReadWrite, etc.)\\n- Labels and annotations for bootstrap policy objects\\n- API group constants for various Kubernetes APIs\\n- ClusterRoles function: Returns default cluster roles\\n- ClusterRoleBindings function: Returns default cluster role bindings\\n\\n**namespace_policy.go** (plugin/pkg/auth/authorizer/rbac/bootstrappolicy/namespace_policy.go):\\n- Defines namespace-scoped roles and bindings for reserved kube-* namespaces\\n- NamespaceRoles function: Returns roles in kube-public, kube-system namespaces\\n- NamespaceRoleBindings function: Returns namespace-scoped bindings\\n\\n**controller_policy.go** (plugin/pkg/auth/authorizer/rbac/bootstrappolicy/controller_policy.go):\\n- Defines roles for Kubernetes controllers (attachdetach-controller, bootstrap-signer, etc.)\\n- buildControllerRoles function: Constructs controller cluster roles and bindings\\n- ControllerRoles function: Returns controller-specific cluster roles\\n- ControllerRoleBindings function: Returns bindings for controller service accounts in kube-system\\n\\n### 6. Escalation Prevention and Policy-Based Storage\\n\\n**escalation_check.go** (pkg/registry/rbac/escalation_check.go):\\n- **EscalationAllowed function** (line 31): Checks if user is in system:masters group (superuser exemption)\\n- **RoleEscalationAuthorized function** (line 54): Checks if user has explicit \\\"escalate\\\" verb permission on roles/clusterroles\\n- **BindingAuthorized function** (line 100): Checks if user has \\\"bind\\\" permission for a specific role reference\\n\\n**Role Storage** (pkg/registry/rbac/role/policybased/storage.go):\\n- **Storage struct**: Wraps StandardStorage with escalation prevention\\n- **Create method** (line 67): Uses ConfirmNoEscalationInternal to prevent privilege escalation\\n- **Update method** (line 80): Similar escalation checks before updates\\n- Allows escalation if EscalationAllowed or RoleEscalationAuthorized returns true\\n\\n**ClusterRole Storage** (pkg/registry/rbac/clusterrole/policybased/storage.go):\\n- **Storage struct**: Wraps StandardStorage with escalation prevention\\n- **Create method** (line 73): Prevents creating roles with rules the user doesn't have\\n- **Update method** (line 93): Prevents privilege escalation in updates\\n- Special handling for AggregationRule which requires cluster-admin privileges\\n\\n**RoleBinding Storage** (pkg/registry/rbac/rolebinding/policybased/storage.go):\\n- **Storage struct**: Wraps StandardStorage with binding authorization\\n- **Create method** (line 70): Checks BindingAuthorized and escalation via ConfirmNoEscalation\\n- Prevents binding to roles with rules the user doesn't have\\n\\n**ClusterRoleBinding Storage** (pkg/registry/rbac/clusterrolebinding/policybased/storage.go):\\n- **Storage struct**: Similar to RoleBinding but cluster-wide\\n- **Create method** (line 69): Checks BindingAuthorized and escalation\\n- **Update method** (line 94): Similar checks for updates\\n\\n**Escalation Validation** (pkg/registry/rbac/validation/rule.go and internal_version_adapter.go):\\n- **ConfirmNoEscalation function** (rule.go:52): Ensures user rules cover the roles being granted\\n- **ConfirmNoEscalationInternal function** (internal_version_adapter.go:27): Converts internal rbac types to v1 for validation\\n\\n### 7. RBAC REST Storage Integration (pkg/registry/rbac/rest/storage_rbac.go)\\n- **RESTStorageProvider struct** (line 61): Registers RBAC storage with the API server\\n- **storage method** (line 81): Creates policy-based storage wrappers for roles, rolebindings, clusterroles, and clusterrolebindings\\n- **PostStartHook method** (line 131): Bootstraps RBAC policies at cluster startup via PolicyData.EnsureRBACPolicy()\\n- **PolicyData struct** (line 143): Holds cluster roles, bindings, namespace roles, and bindings to be created at startup\\n\\n## Authorization Flow Summary\\n\\n1. **API Request** → Reaches authorization layer\\n2. **RBACAuthorizer.Authorize()** → Uses RequestToRuleMapper to check rules\\n3. **DefaultRuleResolver.VisitRulesFor()** → Finds applicable roles/rolebindings for user\\n4. **RuleAllows()** → Checks if any rule matches the request\\n5. **Decision** → Allow/Deny/NoOpinion returned to API server\\n\\nFor mutations on Role/RoleBinding/ClusterRole/ClusterRoleBinding:\\n- Policy-based storage wrappers intercept Create/Update\\n- ConfirmNoEscalation verifies user has permissions for rules being granted\\n- EscalationAllowed/RoleEscalationAuthorized provide superuser/admin bypasses\\n- BindingAuthorized ensures binding permissions are respected\\n\\nThis architecture ensures both flexible authorization and privilege escalation prevention in Kubernetes RBAC.\"\n}\n"},"caller":{"type":"direct"}}],"stop_reason":null,"stop_sequence":null,"usage":{"input_tokens":11,"cache_creation_input_tokens":3397,"cache_read_input_tokens":82922,"cache_creation":{"ephemeral_5m_input_tokens":0,"ephemeral_1h_input_tokens":3397},"output_tokens":3,"service_tier":"standard","inference_geo":"not_available"},"context_management":null},"parent_tool_use_id":null,"session_id":"df2e929d-2b8b-43b0-a8fe-47163161ef62","uuid":"bf0415a1-0112-4313-83e3-c244208273a1"}
